 The Supreme Court on Thursday upheld the cairn-vedanta deal, saying that the Central Government and ongc's decision not to exercise the right of first refusal in the Cairn India stock sale case was a purely forward-looking commercial decision
 nyaayalay ne kaha ki centre va oengisi ne kern india ke share nahin kharidne kaa faisla vibhinn vanijyik tathaa takneekee pahaluon par vichaar karne ke baad kiya or vah pakshon dwaara kiye gaye vanijyik yaa vyapaarik faislon par koi nirnay nahin de saktaa
 a bench of Justices KS Radhakrishnan and Deepak Mishra said, "on the basis of facts and by law, it is our opinion that ONGC and the Government of India have taken a far-reaching commercial and economic decision in the public interest"
 ham yah kehane ko taiyaar nahin hai ki faisla kisi galat manshaa tathaa kisi bahari athwa anuchit uddeshy se prerit tha
 The bench said, "we notice that ONGC and the Government of India have considered various commercial and technical aspects related to the Production Partnership Agreement (PSC), as well as the benefits that ONGC after the Cairn Vedanta deal Had to meet ‚Äô‚Äô The court passed the order on a PIL alleging that there was a clause in the contract between Cairn Group and ONGC that if Cairn Group wants to sell its shares in Cairn India, it must first offer it to ONGC , But the government and ONGC did not exercise this right
 sabhi pahaluon par vichaar karne ke baad nyaayalay kii khandpeeth is nishkarsh par pahunchi ki oengisi dwaara apane pehle inkaar kaa adhikaar (aroefar) kaa istemaal nahin karne kaa faisla samuchit vichaar-vimarsh ke baad kiya gaya
 Accordingly, the report given by SBI Caps after a comprehensive financial analysis also supports ongc's decision
 khandpeeth ne kaha ki adaalaton ko un vanijyik tathaa vyapaarik faislon main hastkshep nahin karnaa chahie jo kisi sanvaidhanik praavdhaanon kaa ulanghan nahin karte hon athwa ve kisi bahari nihitarth yaa anuchit lakshya ke liye nahin liye gaye hon
 The petitioner also alleged that the PSU and the government's decision regarding the deal was taken for reasons other than its worthwhile aspects

 vah sabase badhkar ek kissago he, yani aadhunik yug kaa chaaran yaa kavi
 Ravish started reporting 19 years ago, and recognized from the beginning that television is the medium of anecdote, so Ravish chose the news that was the same as betia
 vaise kisse, jinke charitra apane jaise lagate the, jinaki shuruyaat hoti thi, madhya hota tha, ant hota tha
 This is the secret of Ravish's success as an inventor and advocate of truth, and this is the reason for his huge success as a Magsaysay Award
 television kaa samay ek hi disha main chalata he
 Now, it is common knowledge that time goes on like this, but when we read something, we can leave out some words or paragraphs, so that we can come back and read and understand them later
 yah ateet ko lautaa laane jaisaa he, lekin LIVE news asli vakt main hi ghatati he, ise lautaaya nahin ja saktaa

 raveesh ne is sach ko pahchaan liya, or kissagoi sareekha anoothaa tarika apanaaya, kyonki kisse dekhne waalon ko kisse ke saath-saath baandhe chalate hai
 They are easy to remember, especially in countries like ours, where a large number of people are almost illiterate
 raveesh kii bhashaa or haavbhaav main ve sabhi tarkiben samahit dikhti hai, jo sthapit upanyaaskaaron se lekar filmkaar or lokkalakaar tak apanaate rahe hai

 Journalism's own image is that it is called the fourth pillar of democracy

 The news media empowers citizens through information, so that they can prevent possible encroachments by those in power

 Ravish Kumar deliberately abandoned this traditional method
 vah un logon kaa kissa saamne laana chaahate the, jinka koi naam hi nahin - mazdoor, beghar vidhwaa, kisi gaanv ke skool main mid-de mile kaa intazaar karte bachche, kasaai, bekri vaala yaa mombatiyaan banane vaala
 And Ravish wanted these people to have a name, an identity, because their daily struggle is also as important for democracy as new bills being introduced in Parliament
 raveesh ne in adrishy logon ko hamaari rozmarra kii zindagi main dikhaaya
